Soliciting Opinions on Monetary Issues

Soong Scheduled to Return Home by Ship on the 12th

Hyde Park: Today, the U.S. President temporarily postponed his meeting with monetary advisors to meet with Chinese Minister of Finance T.V. Soong and Chinese Minister Shih Chao-chi. It is reported that the U.S. President's meeting with Soong was to learn the Chinese government's views on the current monetary situation and Soong's impressions of Europe's attempts to stabilize currency. However, after the meeting, those in the President's private residence claimed that no details could be disclosed regarding the conversation and that the topics discussed by both parties would not be revealed. The U.S. President's meeting with monetary advisors will likely be rescheduled for tomorrow. It is reported that the U.S. President has effectively postponed the inflationary monetary policy until the overall price level is stabilized but will continue to closely monitor the monetary situation. (National Telegram, 7th)

(Nanjing) T.V. Soong recently telegraphed Beijing, stating that he has arrived in New York and is scheduled to return home via the Pacific Ocean on the Italian mail ship Conte Rosso from Canada on the 12th, expected to arrive in Shanghai by the end of this month. (Special Dispatch, 8th)

Morgan Silver Company Signs Regulations 16

(New York) The U.S. government's industrial recovery movement is receiving a strong response. Morgan Company today signed temporary regulations stipulating a maximum of 40 working hours per week and a minimum wage of $15 per week. This serves as a starting point for major banks to sign regulations. Soon after, General Motors also announced that all employees would receive a 10% wage increase from August 1st. (Reuters dispatch, 7th)

Significant Progress in U.S. Economic Conditions 17

All Industries Rebounding, Prices Rising

(New York) American economist Babson reported on the U.S. economic situation today, stating that 70% of the increase in U.S. prices is a genuine increase, and 70% of the improvement in U.S. industries is a genuine recovery. The remaining 30% is due to speculation and enthusiasm for greater progress. However, the rise in prices and the progress in industries in such a short period can be described as the fastest ever seen in the United States, especially in July. However, it has now entered a period of irregular price fluctuations, which is why various markets have been sluggish recently. However, this period may not last long. Babson's statement that 70% is genuine progress is based on his various market fluctuation charts and is highly reliable. Before the economic decline began in 1929, Babson had already predicted the collapse of the stock market based on these charts. (National Telegram, 7th)

U.S. Sugar Industry Association Submits Recommendations to the Government 18

Requesting Full Authority to Manage Sales

Difficulties in Reducing Cuban Sugar Imports

(Washington) The U.S. Sugar Industry Association today requested the government to make it the dictator of the beet sugar industry, granting it full authority to manage all sales matters, subject to government supervision. This recommendation by the Association is included in a supplementary sales agreement, which has been approved by all parties in the industry and submitted to the government for approval today. The industry previously submitted a sales agreement stipulating that if Cuban sugar imports could be limited to 1.76 million tons per year, then sugar produced in the U.S. mainland would be reduced to 1.865 million tons. The U.S. government is considering this proposal tonight and attempting to compromise with the Cuban sugar industry's demand for a larger import quota. It is reported that Cuba wants to import 3.5 million tons annually, or at least insists on 2 million tons. However, it is also difficult to reduce Cuban sugar imports because not only is a large portion of the Cuban sugar industry American capital, but it would also reduce U.S. tariff revenue. Currently, Cuban sugar is taxed at two cents per pound. If the minimum amount requested by Cuba is accepted, the annual tax revenue would be one hundred million yuan. Conversely, if the amount proposed by the U.S. Sugar Industry Association is followed, the annual tax revenue would only be 68 million yuan at the current tax rate, resulting in a loss of 32 million yuan. This is a major problem for the treasury deficit, especially during times of financial strain.

(National Telegram, 7th)

India-Japan Conference is Like a Castle in the Air, Japan is Being Played by British Diplomacy 19

Japanese People Greatly Disappointed with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs

Sawada and Terao Have to Postpone Their Departure

(Tokyo) Regarding the Simla conference, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has requested the British government to commit to confirming two essential conditions for the meeting: that the commercial treaty concluded between Japan and India not be changed by the British government and that a temporary agreement be established to avoid being treated as a country without a treaty before a new treaty is established. However, the British government avoided a definite answer in its reply on the 2nd, and it is difficult to expect a quick response. Therefore, the departure of the two representatives, Sawada and Terao, scheduled for August 24th, has to be postponed. There is no hope of concluding negotiations before the expiry date of the current commercial treaty, October 10th. Ambassador Sawada stated that without these two guarantees, the Simla conference would be like a castle in the air. It has been four months since the Ministry of Foreign Affairs announced the termination of the treaty, and it is being manipulated by the clever diplomatic tactics of the British government. Wasting time in such an inconclusive state makes the Simla conference increasingly disadvantageous to Japan. The relevant ministries are extremely concerned about this, and the public is also expressing disappointment with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' handling of the matter. (Dentsu Telegram, 8th)

France Occupies Nine Islands in the South China Sea 20

Britain Expresses No Opposition

(Paris) It is learned that the French government is still awaiting the protest being drafted by the Japanese government regarding the French Navy's occupation of nine small islands. The French government sent a formal notification to the Japanese government three weeks ago regarding the flag-raising occupation of these islands, pointing out that the Japanese company that wanted to operate phosphate mines on the islands had failed and withdrawn in 1925. Therefore, it is now believed that the Japanese government's communication to the French government will be a request for explanation, not a protest. The British government has announced that it does not oppose the French Navy's occupation of the nine small islands because they are not on shipping lanes and have no residents except for a few Chinese fishermen. However, these islands are important for the traffic along the French Vietnamese coastlines and can also serve as a base for seaplanes and submarines. (Reuters dispatch, 7th)

Illegal Negotiations on the Chinese Eastern Railway Again End Without Result 21

Sixth Meeting Discusses Valuation Issues

(Tokyo) The sixth meeting on the transfer of the Chinese Eastern Railway was held on the 4th. This afternoon at 2:00 PM, Vice Minister Ohashi and Soviet Russia's Katzlovsky met again at the official residence of the Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs. The Soviet Russian side made the following statement regarding the meeting on the 4th: The Soviet Russian delegation is striving for the most rapid and smooth progress in these negotiations, demonstrating its sincerity and desire to ensure their success. Especially with regard to the stated value, it is extremely appropriate and fully substantiated, and it specifically expresses the intention to reduce it to 50 million gold rubles. The Soviet Russian delegation immediately proposed a genuine review of all issues related to the sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway. Furthermore, the Manchurian delegation respects the proper handling of existing treaties and considers mutual interests, which has greater significance at this meeting. The Soviet Russian delegation, with the same sincerity, expects to express its intention to achieve the success of the meeting. Furthermore, today's meeting between the two countries' representatives did not involve the issue of calculating gold rubles; it only touched on the issue of valuation. (Dentsu Telegram, 8th)

(Tokyo) The sixth round of negotiations on the Chinese Eastern Railway ended without result because a solution could not be found for the pre-arranged transfer price. Yesterday, Manchurian representative Tadashi Ohashi and Soviet Russian representative Kazlovsky began informal talks on the conversion of rubles, which is the basis for calculating the price. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs, as the mediator, is deeply dissatisfied with the high conversion rate of 1.4 rubles per gold ruble proposed by the Soviet Russian side, dismissing it. Furthermore, the Japan-Russia Fisheries Agreement adopts the principle of converting one ruble to 0.325 Japanese yen, and in 1931, an American insurance company established a conversion agreement with Soviet Russia for 0.35 rubles per ruble. It is said that the Soviet Russian side's figures were not corrected, failing to fulfill the mediator's responsibilities. Furthermore, if the conversion rate is 0.325, then the 250 million rubles proposed by the Soviet Russian side is 81.25 million yen. If it is 0.25, then it is 62.5 million yen, not far from the Manchurian side's proposed 50 million yen. Therefore, the solution to the problem lies in whether a consistent conversion rate can be found. The private consultations between the Russian and Manchurian representatives are highly significant. (Dentsu Telegram, 8th)

(Moscow) During today's meeting, the Manchurian representative read a statement acknowledging the value of the Chinese Eastern Railway to "Manchukuo" but stating that the railway has no value to Soviet Russia. The Russian newspaper Pravda commented on this matter, stating that although the Japanese representative participated in the meeting as an observer, if Japan genuinely intends for the negotiations to succeed, then its mediation will definitely have sufficient influence on the Manchurian representative. If the Manchurian representative insists on the original price of 50 million Japanese yen, and the mediation permitted by the Japanese government ultimately fails to take effect, then it will be known that the Japanese side is not genuinely striving for mediation. Japan's scheme to instigate the breakdown of the meeting, hiding behind the "Manchukuo" independence, cannot deceive anyone. The Russian representative's declaration at the last meeting has already expressed the Soviet Russian side's readiness to facilitate the success of the negotiations. Now, it only remains for those who control Japanese policy to choose whether or not to support the completion of the negotiations. (Reuters dispatch, 7th)

Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs Establishes Three New Bureaus to Strengthen Diplomatic Array 22

The Osaka Mainichi Shimbun reported on August 2nd that since the failure of the World Economic Conference, the economic nationalism and regional economic alliances of various countries have become increasingly acute. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs, in view of the inevitable trend in the world, is striving for "economic diplomacy" and "establishment of commercial rights." It has already prepared principled and concrete plans. In response to the trend of nationalistic alliances, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs will reorganize its existing Europe-America Bureau into the Europe Bureau and newly establish several bureaus to focus on various aspects. As for the responsibilities of the American Bureau, it will be responsible for the affairs of American citizens and serve as a symbol of the close relationship with the United States. At the same time, it will also study measures to revise maritime treaties and address military issues. In addition to the above, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has also established a committee with a budget of 40 million yen for the Asia Bureau and the International Cultural Bureau to enhance its diplomatic capabilities.

Page 9

Current Commentary

Training Civilians in Urban Air Defense 23

A statement by Xu Peigen, Director of the Aviation Administration, regarding the development of the air force was published in this newspaper on the 5th. It emphasized the importance of training civilians in urban air defense, with the first large-scale civilian air defense exercise scheduled to be held in Nanjing in sixteen months, followed by a second exercise in Shanghai twelve months later, and a third in Tianjin. The intention seems to be to complete the air defense arrangements in China's vulnerable areas within three years. It is believed by world military experts that the Second World War will break out in 1936, three years from now.

Urban air defense exercises involve matters handled by military authorities and preparations to be made by the people. The establishment of an air defense command and the fulfillment of the qualifications required by the air defense commander are matters that should be handled by the military authorities. Disseminating knowledge of aerial warfare and cultivating agile and orderly habits are the preparations that the people should make. The former is not the subject of this article, so I will briefly describe the latter.

The awesomeness of aerial warfare lies in the intensity of the suffering it causes and the speed with which enemy aircraft arrive. The rubble in Zhabei still remains, and we should have recognized the power of the air force. As for its speed, modern aircraft fly at a speed of 180 to 240 kilometers per hour, with an average speed of over 60 meters per second (equivalent to 200 old feet). For example, the distance of 16 kilometers between Shanghai and Wusong is only a five-minute flight. If the citizens are not trained in air defense, the warning sound will not have stopped, and the enemy aircraft will have arrived, dropping explosive bombs, and disaster will strike. Therefore, urban air defense usually establishes air defense monitoring posts with reconnaissance aircraft 120 to 130 kilometers away from the defense center. So that the city can hear the warning, the defensive air force can fly out to meet the enemy, and the citizens can immediately extinguish the lights and stop all actions to avoid becoming targets for enemy aircraft. The air defense command can also carry out camouflage operations or disguise targets that the enemy aircraft would want to obtain in open areas to exhaust their bombing power.

Regardless of how quickly the air defense authorities carry out camouflage work or how the air defense forces engage the enemy, the residents of the city under air attack should complete their evacuation within twenty minutes of hearing the alarm at the latest. This evacuation includes: (1) Immediately extinguish all city lights in accordance with the lighting management regulations. (2) Quickly enter the pre-designated bunkers. (3) Stop all actions that may be visible to enemy aircraft, even to avoid any shadows, smoke, or dust being detected in the city. During urban air defense exercises, the duties of the air defense police are particularly important. It is not easy to have a large group of chaotic and panicked citizens orderly and quickly complete all the things they should do under air defense regulations in an instant without good command and supervision. Chinese people have a habit of shouting for their wives and children when they encounter emergencies and often rush to be the first. All of these are things that should not happen when being attacked by enemy aircraft. If a large team of trained air defense police is not dispatched to patrol the districts, the problem of everyone crowding one boat is bound to happen.

Shanghai has already suffered from Japanese aircraft attacks during the January 28th Incident last year. However, for more than a year, we have only seen news of air defense exercises in Tokyo, and we ourselves have not received training in air raid evacuation after suffering huge sacrifices. Now, on the occasion of the Director of the Aviation Administration's announcement of the timing of air defense exercises, I will briefly describe what I know. I deeply hope that domestic military experts can do more to increase the people's knowledge of air defense.

Non-Stop Long-Distance Flight Creates New Record for Aviators 24

Departing from New York, Landing in Syria

Traveling 6,000 Miles in Fifty-Four Hours

Not Letting British Officers Dominate

Baghdad, Reuters, 7th: French aviators Rossi and Codou landed in Rayak, Syria (Greenwich time) at 4:25 PM today. From the time of their departure from New York to the time of landing, they flew in the air for a total of 54 hours and 45 minutes, covering a distance of 5,911 and a half miles, exceeding the record of 5,340 miles set by British Royal Air Force officers Gayford and Nicolay in February last year by 571 and a half miles.

Progressing Smoothly Along the Way 25

Paris, Reuters, 7th

During their flight from New York to Syria, covering nearly 6,000 miles, French aviators Codou and Rossi sent wireless telegrams from time to time, reporting on the situation. After leaving New York at 5:41 AM on Saturday, the St. John's radio station in New Brunswick immediately received a wireless telegram stating that the flight was proceeding smoothly. Less than an hour after departure, they flew over Newfoundland and headed towards the ocean. They flew through adverse weather for 20 hours and flew over the French ports of Cherbourg and Le Bourget airport at 6 PM on Sunday evening. Two hours later, they telegraphed that they were proceeding urgently and hoping to reach Aleppo in Turkey, Asia.

Russian Aviator Performs Amazing Feats in the Air 26

Falling 20,000 Feet from an Airplane

Opening a Parachute and Landing Safely on the Ground

Leningrad, Reuters, 7th: Today, Russian aviator Gifdudimov fell 20,000 feet from an airplane here before pulling the cord to open his parachute. Landing safely on the ground only 2,000 feet from the ground, he set a new record. The previous record was held by Trallum, who jumped from an airplane at an altitude of 20,000 feet on the 5th of this year, falling to 17,500 feet before opening his parachute. His landing point was about 5 miles from the airfield. Trallum now only holds the record for low jumping, which he set by jumping off the Pasadena Bridge in California, only 150 feet from the ground.

Korean Female Aviator Dies in Plane Crash 27

Tokyo, 8th Dispatch from Japan Federation – Korean female aviator Park Kyung-won, en route from Haneda Airfield to Changchun, crashed and died in a mountainous area in Shizuoka Prefecture.

Atami, 8th Dispatch from Dentsu – At 8:00 AM this morning, a crashed airplane was discovered by villagers in a mountain area of Tagamura, Tagata County, Shizuoka Prefecture. Firefighters, youth groups, and veterans mobilized upon hearing the news. The airplane was completely destroyed, making rescue impossible. Investigation revealed that it belonged to Korean female aviator Miss Park Kyung-won. Miss Park herself tragically died.

Starting from Munich, Vienna, Greece, and Achensee, at 3:30 PM (local time) on Monday, the plane reached Aleppo, setting a new record for non-stop long-distance flight. French Volle radio station intercepted a telegram stating that the plane was turning south, following the railway line towards Damascus. If all goes well, it is planned to land at Rayak, fifty miles northwest of Fuma in French Syria, at dusk.

Commendable Achievement 28

New York, 7th Dispatch from Havas – American aviator Chamberlain, one of the first to fly across the Atlantic, commented on the new long-distance direct flight record (over 9,300 kilometers) set by French aviators Codos and Rossi, saying that Codos and Rossi encountered severe weather in the Atlantic, yet they were able to break the record of British aviators Gayford and Nicholetts, making their achievement even more commendable than that of Gayford and Nicholetts.

British Newspapers Laud Extensively 29

London, 8th Dispatch from Havas – British newspapers extensively praised the French aviators Codos and Rossi for breaking the British aviators' record, without any jealousy. For example, The Daily Telegraph, representing common opinion, stated that the flight of Codos and Rossi was a remarkable feat, and aviators from all countries expressed great admiration for the two without hesitation.

Brief Biographies of Codos and Rossi 30

Although Codos and Rossi were unable to reach the Persian Gulf directly, their flight through the extremely difficult conditions of the Atlantic Ocean and their eventual success was truly extraordinary. Codos was born in May 1896, participated in the European War, and served in the air force. In 1924, he joined United Airlines as a pilot. Rossi was born in 1901 and obtained his pilot's license in 1926. He flew many times with the late famous French aviator Le Bris. The aircraft they flew was a monoplane with a wing area of 81 square meters, equipped with three engines producing a total of 650 horsepower. It had twelve fuel tanks with a total capacity of 8,000 liters, capable of continuous flight for 70 hours, and a range of 12,600 kilometers. Aviation Minister Gutaud immediately sent a telegram of congratulations after Codos and Rossi landed, and also congratulated the aircraft designer, Mr. Bleriot, and the manager of the engine manufacturing plant.

(Havas Agency)

Jiangsu Provincial Government Requests Exemption from Disciplinary Action

The matter of disciplinary action against political officials other than those selected by election is within the purview of the Political Officials Disciplinary Committee. Another Border Conflict Between Germany and Austria 73

German Labor Corps Shoots and Kills an Austrian Patrol Officer

Austrian Patrol Responds with Gunfire, Detaining Four

German Government Rejects British and French Intervention 74

▲ Reuters, Berlin, 7th – Britain and France, regarding the German National Socialist Party's radio broadcasts and leaflet drops in Austria, have sent similar notes to the German government, stating that the actions of the German Party are contrary to existing treaties. The German government has now responded, denying any breach of treaty and stating that it deems such intervention in the German-Austrian dispute to be unacceptable. Furthermore, according to the German Public Gazette, the German government does not understand how the Four-Power Pact could be invoked in such an event. From the German perspective, Germany has not violated any treaty. German newspapers also carry officially authorized articles criticizing the Dollfuss government (Austria) for disregarding the moral and spiritual changes of the Austrian people. The articles also criticize France and its allies for allowing Austria to establish an auxiliary police force of 18,000, which is contrary to the spirit of the Four-Power Pact.

▲ Havas, Paris, 7th – The Times published an editorial on the German-Austrian situation, stating, "The tension in German-Austrian relations is attracting great attention from various countries, as evidenced by Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss's formal visit to Italian Prime Minister Mussolini. Mussolini's assistance to Dollfuss in maintaining Austrian independence makes international observers believe in the sincerity of Italy's assistance to Austria. How Berlin will react is also of great interest to us. In short, there are currently multifaceted diplomatic actions aimed at clarifying the atmosphere in Central Europe." The Times concluded that the current negotiations are aimed at opening up a situation so that the German-Austrian dispute can be resolved before it becomes a conflict. The Times believes that immediately submitting the German-Austrian issue to the Council of the League of Nations for review would be a major inconvenience because German nationalism is currently on the rise. Submitting the issue to the League of Nations would publicly declare German responsibility to the world, which may provoke a fierce reaction from the German people. The Times also stated, "However, if Germany fails to understand the warnings from all parties, the major powers can only submit the case to the Council of the League of Nations for review in accordance with the letter and spirit of the League of Nations Covenant and will no longer intervene in negotiations. The Council will also only take appropriate measures in accordance with the text and spirit of the League of Nations Covenant."

▲ Reuters, Vienna, 7th – One of the Austrian patrol officers on the Austrian-German border near Kufstein in Salzburg Province was shot and killed today. The shooter's clothing was similar to that worn by the German volunteer labor corps currently stationed across the border in Kiefersfelden. Austrian authorities have dispatched additional auxiliary police to the scene of the incident and established a line of sentries along the border, cutting off traffic near the scene. It is reported that while the Austrian patrol officers were serving within their boundary, fifteen individuals wearing steel helmets suddenly launched an attack, firing a volley of shots. One Austrian patrol officer was shot in the chest and fell to the ground. His companions immediately returned fire, and the attackers fled, and it is unknown if there were any injuries. The Austrian people are currently very agitated, believing that this attack was prearranged. Four individuals have been arrested, including three members of the Austrian Social Democratic Party. On the 3rd of this month, a similar incident occurred, but no one was injured at that time. It is now believed that the German attack was an act of revenge because a German was loitering near the border, and when Austrian soldiers ordered him to stop and he did not comply, they opened fire and shot him.

▲ Reuters, Vienna, 7th – According to Munich sources, the Austrian policeman who was shot and killed while patrolling the Austrian-German border was named Schwanninger. This matter seems to have international implications, as Britain and France recently sent notes to the German Foreign Ministry protesting the National Socialist Party's propaganda in Austria. It is reported that the German reply has now been issued, stating that Germany does not wish to discuss the matter. Austrian troops are now rushing to the border, and traffic is now closed.

▲ Guomin, Vienna, 7th – As the conflict between the Austrian National Socialist Party and the Dollfuss government intensifies, a very large swastika was painted on the side of a mountain near Innsbruck, visible throughout the town. The police then searched various public bathhouses and arrested thirty members of the National Socialist Party.

Draft Constitution for the Separation of India and Burma Announced 79

▲Havas, London, 8th - The constitutional reform plan for Burma, drafted by the Secretary of State for India, Mr. Hoare, has been announced. This plan, which applies when Burma separates from India, will be studied by a joint committee. The joint committee, established to study Indian constitutional reform, is scheduled to meet on the 13th to decide the fate of Burma. Mr. Hoare's draft stipulates that the administrative power of Burma is to be held by the Governor, representing the British monarch, and assisted by a cabinet responsible to the parliament. The parliament is divided into two houses, an upper house with forty-five members and a lower house with one hundred and thirty-eight members. The cabinet's power extends to all kinds of affairs, except for national defense, foreign affairs, and religious authority, which are held by the Governor.

Japan with the Scent of War (Japan Correspondence) 80

Strengthening Naval and Army Forces to Deal with the United States and the Soviet Union

Important Cities in the Kanto Area Rehearse Air Defense

Everyone knows that the Japanese also claim to be a maritime nation like the British Isles. However, Britain has always maintained its identity as a maritime nation because it developed early, so almost all of the world's undeveloped land and abundant natural resources have been occupied and developed by the British Empire. Therefore, its colonies are all over the world, and its military strength is naturally focused on the navy. Japan, on the other hand, is the opposite. Although it is a maritime nation, it concentrates all its attention on the continent. Its two foreign wars, the Sino-Japanese War and the Russo-Japanese War, were both decided by land battles. Therefore, in the past, before the era of Aritomo Yamagata, the navy was under the command of the General Staff Headquarters. In other words, the army warlords led the navy warlords. It was not until Yamagata was about to die that the Naval Command was separated from the command of the General Staff Headquarters and became independent.

Until recently, the vanguard of Japanese imperialism was still the army. For example, it was the army that provoked the September 18th Mukden Incident, and it was the army that seized the territory of the three northeastern provinces. Although it was the navy that provoked the Shanghai Incident, in the end, it still mobilized more than four divisions of the army to regain its face. As for the invasion of Rehe and the attack on eastern Tianjin, it was entirely dependent on the army. From one perspective, the Japanese army can be said to be at its peak, invincible. Therefore, it is truly considered the favored son of heaven in the country. Coupled with the promotion of the veterans' associations, it considers itself invincible. However, the enemy it has found is China, which is said to have many soldiers but lacks modern weapons and equipment. In fact, its victory is only the victory of weapons that are one level higher, and not a victory of spirit. Its weapons are only slightly better than China's. If it were to compare with continental military powers such as France, it would be a case of a small sorcerer meeting a great one. Even compared with the emerging Soviet Union, it feels inferior. First, in terms of modern mechanized units, the entire Japanese army has only two regiments, while the Soviet Union has four mechanized divisions. Second, in terms of aircraft, the entire Japanese army and navy have only about 1,200 aircraft. Adding the 150 civilian aircraft, it still does not reach 1,500. The Soviet Union has four times as many, and the United States has eight times as many. In the naval sphere, Japan also feels quite satisfied, because in terms of naval tonnage figures, it ranks first except for Britain and the United States. Although seizing Honolulu is not sufficient, maintaining traffic in the East China Sea and the West Pacific is more than enough. Moreover, it has its own special defense and attack capabilities. In the naval aspect, its first strength is its submarines. They are new, well-equipped, have long endurance, and strong attack power. Not only is the United States far behind, but even Britain, the king of the seas, is amazed. The second is heavy and light cruisers. Although the number of ships is less than that of the United States, the speed and the range of the guns are higher than those of the United States. Therefore, its army and navy are sufficient to deal with both the United States and the Soviet Union.

However, its main shortcomings at present, as mentioned above,

apart from mechanized units (because mechanized units can only be used on land, then they are only useful in the theaters of the three northeastern provinces or Mongolia, and only during the war with the Soviet Union, and have little other use), it has another major shortcoming, which is the air force, because the air force can take off from aircraft carriers at sea, can use islands as bases, and can also use the Shandong Peninsula or the vicinity of Shanghai as bases to attack major Japanese cities. Therefore, the Japanese military is very vigilant against foreign air raids. Especially after the recent success of flying across the ocean, it is even more vigilant. It envisions, if foreign aircraft were to attack, what should Japan do? Therefore, it pays great attention to air defense, especially in major cities such as Tokyo, Osaka, Kyoto, and Kobe, and strives to build air defense facilities. In addition to active defenses such as anti-aircraft guns and sound locators, there are also passive defenses such as smoke screens, traffic control, lighting management, and poison gas and medical assistance. On the 20th of this month, air defense exercises will be held in important cities in the Kanto area. Twelve aircraft will be formed into three teams to act as enemy aircraft, flying to Tokyo to drop bombs and poison gas. On the defense side, a defense command headquarters has been established within the Tokyo Metropolitan Police Department. The former commander of the First Division, Mr. Hayashi Sen-no-suke, is the commander of the exercise security. Civilian youth groups will all be mobilized to assist in various passive defenses. At 1:00 PM, a warning of an air raid was received. The Guard Division and the First Division were fully mobilized and deployed in all important locations. Of course, the Ministry of the Army was full of the scent of war. The area near the Ministry of the Army was covered with dense smoke screens, and the poison gas team and the fire brigade were all ready for action. In short, everything was in a state of war, and the management of lighting was the only stimulant to promote civilian tension. From the above exercises, we can see Japan's active preparations for war and its emphasis on air defense. (July 28, 1933, Tokyo)

Feng Yuxiang Returns the Administration of Chahar 81

The Military and Political Affairs of Chahar Are All Under the Control of Song Zheyuan

General Feng Will Leave Zhangjiakou and Move to Zhangbei

Special Dispatch from Beiping - The situation in Chahar has taken a sudden turn. Feng sent a representative, Liu Zhizhou, to Shacheng to visit Pang Bingxun and Guan Linzheng, stating that Feng was willing to accept the four principles of Wang Jingwei and Chiang Kai-shek's telegram and the three measures proposed by He Yingqin. He hoped that Song Zheyuan would meet with Feng's representative in Shacheng to end the military situation and return the administration of Chahar. The Beiping authorities received Pang and Guan's telegrams and immediately invited Song and others to discuss the matter. It was decided that Song would first go to Chahar to handle the matter. Song, accompanied by Qin Dechun, Jiang Bocheng, Xiong Bin, and Feng's representatives Deng Zhexin and Li Xin, went north at 8:00 AM yesterday and arrived in Shacheng at 1:00 PM. They met with the frontline generals Pang Bingxun and Xu Tingyao and held brief discussions. When Feng heard that Song was going to Chahar, he sent Tong Lingge and his chief of staff, Qiu Shanning, to Xiahuayuan to meet with Song. Song rested briefly in Shacheng and then accompanied Qin Dechun to Xiahuayuan to wait for Tong and others. At around 10:00 PM, Tong and others arrived in Xiahuayuan. Song discussed matters with Tong and others in the car and then went to Shacheng together to discuss everything in detail. After the meeting, Tong and others returned to Zhangjiakou to report. Song Zheyuan and Jiang Bocheng sent a telegram to Beiping this morning, reporting that the negotiations were satisfactory and that peace was hopeful. Xiong Bin also returned to Beiping at 5:00 PM today (the 6th), reporting on the proceedings. Song Zheyuan will temporarily stay in Shacheng to take charge of everything. Two regiments of Song's department, Feng Zhian's division, set off to the Ping Sui Line today to take over the defense. At 1:00 PM today, Feng issued a circular telegram, returning the administration of Chahar. After the circular telegram was issued, Feng heard that he would leave Zhangjiakou and move to Zhangbei, which is 125 li away from Zhangjiakou. Before Song returns to Chahar, local security will be temporarily maintained by Tong Lingge in the name of the Chahar Provincial Garrison Commander. Song's troops will gradually move to take over the defense. (Feng's circular telegram can be found in this newspaper's special dispatch on the 6th)

There are two reasons for the sudden change in the Chahar situation: (1) The situation between the two sides was tense and urgent. If they did not each take a step back, a tragic fratricidal conflict would inevitably occur. (2) The Japanese and puppet troops have again fallen into Duolun, and the Chahar vehicle is in danger. The bandits have penetrated deeply and it is urgent to unite against the invaders. Feng, under internal and external pressure, resolutely requested Song to return to Chahar and return the administration. The authorities, since Feng had made concessions, should act in good faith and meet frankly, ordering Song to return to Chahar and resolve the situation peacefully. The Chahar affair, which has been in dispute for several months, can now be brought to a close. (August 6th)

Post-War Reconstruction in the War Zone is Extremely Difficult (Achieved) 82

Bandits are Like Hair, and the People are Destitute

County Magistrates' Orders Do Not Leave the County Seat

Preparing to Organize Local Militias to Assist in Clearing the Countryside

Special Dispatch from Beiping - Most of the war zones have been taken over, with the exception of Qian'an, Zunhua, Funing, and Dushan Xinglong, which are outside the Great Wall, which have not been successfully taken over. The puppet state in Dushan and Xinglong counties has already set up another county government, and it is feared that it will be difficult to go and take over in fact. Funing, Qian'an, and Zunhua counties have also been unable to go because puppet troops are still entrenched there. Qian'an County Magistrate Lu Qingchen is still staying in Tangshan. Funing County Magistrate Liu Xingpei went to Funing to take over, but was blocked by puppet troops. He telegraphed the provincial government, requesting Li Jichun to send personnel to assist. The provincial government has instructed Xue Zhiheng to inform Li Jichun to assist. There are quite a few puppet troops in the Qian'an area, and they are trying to disband them, or seek to transport them out of the pass. Japanese and puppet troops are mixed in Zunhua County. The Japanese army has a warehouse there, which has not yet been moved, and the garrison has not been withdrawn. The county magistrate of the county, Pei Huanxing, is stranded in Tianjin, and it is difficult to predict when the takeover will take place.

The Japanese army announced that it would withdraw from all routes from the 4th and complete the withdrawal by the 8th. On the Beining Line, all the Kwantung Army east of Changli began to be transported out of Shanhaiguan on the 4th. The guard troops originally stationed along the line will continue to be stationed as usual, as permitted by the Boxer Protocol. On the Pingbei side, the headquarters of the Suzuki Brigade in Miyun began to send troops to Gubeikou. About 100 members of the 8th Field Artillery Regiment withdrew to Rehe yesterday (the 5th) and went to Chengde. The Japanese army in Miyun City will not be completely withdrawn, and plans to leave twenty or thirty people to be stationed for a long time. As for the important places inside the Great Wall passes, such as Nantianmen, Saheqiao, Jianchangying, and Shimenzhai, troops will be stationed and will not be withdrawn.

Since the war zones were taken over, the Japanese army has been causing various troubles, violating the spirit of the truce agreement. In short, (1) the Japanese army in the war zone refuses to withdraw completely, (2) Linyu County Town is not allowed to be taken over, (3) interfering in administration, (4) the Beining Line requires conditions for traffic. The Beiping authorities are compromising and negotiating with the Japanese army repeatedly, but have not been able to resolve the matter satisfactorily. The main issue for Huang Fu's trip south this time is to negotiate the diplomatic policy of North China and to solve the various difficult problems in the takeover of the war zone.

The puppet troops of Li Jichun's department within the war zone have been reorganized. The takeover committee member Xue Zhiheng, who was in Tangshan to negotiate the reorganization, returned to Tianjin last night, visited Yu Xuezhong, and reported on the reorganization process. A total of 4,000 officers and soldiers were retained in the reorganized department. The new salary will be paid by the provincial government from August onwards. Yu Xuezhong, believing that the reorganization of the department has been completed, specially instructed Xue Zhiheng to inform Li that since the department has been reorganized, it will be a national force in the future. He hoped that he would pay attention to discipline, maintain local order, and suppress bandits in order to secure the people. The department of Shi Yousan was originally scheduled to go to Yutian to await reorganization, but due to certain relations, it has not yet been transferred. The disposal of the department is still under negotiation.

Within the war zone, in addition to the puppet troops of Li Jichun and Shi Yousan, small groups of scattered bandits are as numerous as hairs. After the reorganization of Li's department, the scattered bandits still occupy various counties, towns, and villages, raping, looting, and making the people destitute. The counties that have been taken over have only taken over the county seat, and have not yet found a way to maintain order in the countryside. Therefore, the strength of the county magistrates cannot reach beyond the city walls. Scattered bandits cannot be suppressed, and all post-war reconstruction cannot proceed. The area of the war zone is extremely large, and the army is limited to the agreement and cannot be stationed there. The only force that can be used to suppress bandits and maintain order is the 8,000 special police, which is actually very difficult. Regarding the post-war reconstruction in the war zone, the authorities are preparing relief through the War Zone Relief Committee on the one hand, and striving to clear the countryside to secure the local area on the other. It is impossible to clear the countryside solely by relying on special police. It is planned to organize local militias to assist in the work, which is currently being planned.

The traffic on the Beining Line has not yet been realized. Recently, the Japanese army in the east began to withdraw, and it was scheduled to open the line on the 8th. Beforehand, the two sides held a meeting in Yuguan to discuss all the procedures in detail. Our representative Yin Tong and Beining Line representative Xu Ji went the other day, but the Japanese unexpectedly demanded that the Beining Line's trains go directly to Shenyang, and the puppet Fengshan Line's trains also go directly to Beiping. Our side believes that such an arrangement would be tantamount to implicitly recognizing the puppet state, which is of great importance. Therefore, the Yuguan meeting could not be held, and the problem of traffic is also difficult to solve. (August 6th)

Continued Report on the Shaanxi Flood 83

Floods Throughout Guanzhong

Hail Also Fell in Northern Shaanxi

Xi'an Correspondence - The floods in our province have been reported in previous news. Recently, there are thirteen more disaster areas that have been reported or not reported by various counties. It can truly be called an unprecedented disaster. The disaster reports from various counties are recorded as follows:

Xianyang 84

In Xianyang, on the afternoon of July 23, dark clouds were dense and heavy rain poured down, with the water level on the ground reaching several feet. Walls collapsed, houses tilted, and countless people and animals died. Especially in the northern plains of the county, the water rushed down violently, and all the low-lying areas were flooded. The lush autumn seedlings were all washed away. The drought has not ended, and the rain disaster has occurred again. Woe to our people, how will they live?

Fufeng 85

In Fufeng, on the night of July 20, black clouds were everywhere and heavy rain poured down, filling the houses and collapsing many walls. In addition, the mountain water flooded, and the ditches were full. On the night of the 22nd, there was continuous heavy rain, like a waterfall, with the water level on the ground reaching three feet. The autumn crops were all submerged, and the villages became a swamp, a vast expanse of water. The roads were cut off. At this time when the drought has just ended, a flood has come again. The future of the people of Fufeng is really difficult to live.

Wugong 86

In Wugong, on July 20, during the heavy rain, the water from the Qiwei and Moyu rivers in the county suddenly burst, and all the grass sheds, melon huts, clothes, and autumn seedlings along the riverbanks for three or four li were completely gone. Thousands of electric poles were washed away. It is estimated that 40 qing of autumn crops were destroyed on both sides of the Mo River, and more than 20 qing of autumn crops were flooded on both sides of the Wei River. The Qi River is the main river in the county, and about 150-160 qing of farmland were destroyed on both sides of the river. A total of more than 200 qing of autumn crops were destroyed, and countless thatched huts, grass sheds, and clothes were lost.

Hua County 87

In Hua County, there was continuous rain a few days ago, and the flood submerged tens of li of land. Many people and livestock died. Similarly, on the north bank of the Wei River, the river water has risen sharply due to continuous rain in recent days, and many acres of autumn crops have been submerged. Local people have petitioned the provincial authorities to provide relief.

Sanyuan 88

On the evening of July 20, there was thunder and lightning, and heavy rain all night, causing a mountain flood. At dawn, the water volume of the Kouzhuo River in our county suddenly rose by eight or nine zhang, surpassing the bridge surface of the Long Bridge, which was built by Wen Gongyi during the Ming Dynasty, and was seven zhang and two chi high. This is a major flood unseen in hundreds of years, and an unprecedented disaster. The residents' fields and properties along the river were all washed away. In total, the reported number of men and women drowned in various districts is about hundreds, and the amount of land washed away is no less than thousands of qing.

Jingyang 89

On the nights of July 20 and 22, there were strong winds and heavy rain, which did not stop all night. The walls in the city and suburbs were several feet deep in water. Because of the rain and mountain floods, the Zhiyu and Qingyu areas along the river became a swamp. Villages, houses, fields, and autumn seedlings were all submerged. The water was so fierce that it reached a height of more than one zhang on the ground. People could not escape and many men and women drowned.

Fu County 90

From noon on July 2, there was continuous rain for seven days and nights. The fields in the east and west rivers were all washed away. In other places, due to continuous rain, the ditches were full, and the streams rose sharply. Many public and private houses and walls in the city and countryside collapsed.

Chunhua 91

In Chunhua, on the evening of July 21, there was heavy rain and mountain water rose sharply. The water in each ditch was several zhang high, and the water on the ground was also several feet high. Wherever the water flowed, houses, fields, livestock, and trees were washed away. Many people were drowned in the county. The flood was particularly severe in the Fangli area of the second district of the county. It is difficult to investigate in detail the damage to houses, lives, and property in the more than 80 villages that were flooded.

Suide 92

On June 9, 10, 15, 29, etc., there were strong winds, thunder, lightning, and hail, as large as chicken eggs, piled up to more than one chi. The summer and autumn seedlings, melons, vegetables, etc. in 135 villages were all damaged.

Yanchang 93

On June 19, there were dark clouds, thunder, lightning, strong winds, and heavy rain mixed with hail, as large as chicken eggs and as small as walnuts. In an instant, cotton, soybeans, etc. were destroyed. The future of the people's livelihood has reached a dead end.

Hengshan 94

More than 50 villages in the first, second, third, and fifth districts, from June 11 to 23, had continuous hail, as large as peaches, fists, and bowls. All the summer crops, autumn seedlings, and melons and vegetables were completely damaged. The people cried to the heavens and the earth, and the misery was unbearable to hear.

Jia County 95

In Jia County, from June 6 to 20, whenever the year arrived, there were strong winds and rain, and continuous hail, as large as chicken eggs. The autumn seedlings were destroyed, and the water accumulated on the ground was one chi deep. It took three or four days to completely dissipate.

Qingjian 96

Qingjian suffered a very large hail disaster on July 19. Heavy rain also poured down, and the hail was more than one inch thick. All the seedlings were destroyed. The people's livelihood was hopeless, and they all fled to other places. The tragic situation was unbearable to speak of. (August 4th)

Confession of Captured Bandits on the Composition of Bandit Army 97

Each Army Corps is Smaller than a National Army Division

The Blockade of the Bandit Areas is a Fatal Blow Nanchang Correspondence - The highest military authority recently obtained a very detailed account of the internal military organization of the Red Bandits from a senior Red Bandit member who surrendered, □□□. It details the number of puppet armies and puppet divisions under each puppet army corps, the number of men and guns in each puppet army and puppet division, and their combat strength. Although the bandit army has designated numbers, the so-called army corps is even smaller than a National Army division. Moreover, there have been many deaths in previous battles. According to the confession, several army and division commanders have also been killed in action, and the situation below is even more imaginable. Moreover, after the bandit areas were tightly blockaded, supplies were cut off, and there was a severe shortage of weapons and ammunition, which was a fatal blow to them. The confession of the senior member is as follows:

The Red Bandits take Jiangxi as their main base of operations, so their internal organization is relatively tight. In terms of military affairs, there is a Military Commission, with Zhu De as chairman and Peng Dehuai and Wang Jiaxiang as deputies. All the Red Bandits in Jiangxi are organized into the First Front Army, with Zhu De as the commander-in-chief and Zhou Enlai as the political commissar. They are also organized into three puppet army corps: the First, Third, and Fifth. The contents of each army corps are as follows:

Puppet First Army Corps 98

Commander-in-chief Lin Biao, political commissar Nie Rongzhen. The army corps is divided into three armies: the Third, Fourth, and Eleventh. The puppet Third Army Commander is Xu Yangang, and the political commissar is Zhu Rui. This army is better armed and has about 4,000 men, responsible for encirclement. The army is divided into three divisions: the Seventh, Eighth, and Ninth, with the Seventh Division being the strongest in combat. The puppet Fourth Army Commander is Zhou Kun, who is as timid as a woman and does not say a word all day. He is brave and good at fighting. The political commissar is Luo Ruiqing, and the chief of staff is Li Yu.

This army has good weapons and combat strength, and is brave in charging. In every battle, it undertakes many attack missions, with about 5,000 men. The army is divided into three divisions: the Tenth, Eleventh, and Twelfth, with the Tenth and Twelfth Divisions being the strongest in combat. The puppet Tenth Division Commander Chen Guang is the bravest, and has been killed in action. The political commissar is Li Xijiu. This division has 28, 29, and 30 regiments. The puppet Eleventh Division Commander is Wu, who has been killed in action. The political commissar is Liu Yaxiu. This division has 31, 32, and 33 regiments. The puppet Twelfth Division Commander is Liu Haiyun, and the political commissar is Liu Yan. This division has 34, 35, and 36 regiments. The puppet Eleventh Army only has the 31st Division. This division was originally the 13th Division of the puppet Fourth Army, with good weapons and more than 2,000 men.

Puppet Third Army Corps 99

Commander-in-chief Peng Dehuai, political commissar Xi Daiyuan, under the jurisdiction of the Seventh Army and the First, Second, and Third Divisions. The Seventh Army Commander is Zhang Xilong, and the political commissar is Yue Shaohua. He is in charge of the 19th, 20th, and 21st Divisions. The names of the division commanders are unknown, but the First Division Commander is Peng Shaohui, the Second Division Commander is Deng Guoqing, and the Third Division Commander is Peng Quan'ao. This army corps has about 6,000 men and 4,800-4,900 guns.

Puppet Fifth Army Corps 100

The commander-in-chief was originally Ji Zhendong, under the jurisdiction of the Thirteenth, Fourteenth, and Fifteenth Armies. The Thirteenth Army Commander is Dong Zhentang, the Fourteenth Army Commander is Zhao Bosheng, and the Fifteenth Army Commander is Huang Yuezhong. When they invaded Fujian, Ji and Huang were imprisoned, and Dong Zhentang was appointed commander-in-chief. The Fourteenth Army was cancelled and merged into the Thirteenth Army. The Fifteenth Army of the army corps was exchanged with the Third Army of the First Army Corps for surveillance purposes. Therefore, the jurisdiction of this army corps became the Third and Thirteenth Armies. In the Battle of Shuikou, this army corps suffered the greatest losses. Zhu and Mao deeply felt that the mixed use of the north and south armies was ineffective, so they reorganized again, and the Thirteenth and Fifteenth Armies were still organized into the Fifth Army Corps, while the Third Army was returned to the First Army Corps. The current commander-in-chief is still Dong Zhentang. The Thirteenth Army Commander Zhao Bosheng has been killed in action (in the Battle of Huangshidu), and the successor is unknown. The Fifteenth Army Commander is Li Qingyun, or Zuo Quan. The entire army corps has a total of more than 4,000 men.

Various Pseudo-Independent Armies 101

In addition, there are the 12th, 21st, 22nd, and 23rd/24th Armies. The 12th Army Commander is Zhang Zongxun, the Political Commissar is Huang Su, and it governs the 34th, 35th, and 36th Divisions. The 34th Division Commander is Qing Geshen, the 35th Division Commander is Yang Rukun, the 36th Division Commander is unknown, and the entire army is approximately over 2,000 people with over 2,000 rifles. The 21st Army is unknown, the number of troops is also over 2,000, with over 1,000 rifles. The 22nd Army Commander is Luo Binghui, the Political Commissar is Tan Zheng, governing the 64th, 65th, and 66th Divisions, with approximately over 3,000 people and over 2,000 rifles. The 23rd Army Commander is Wei Xiean, the Political Commissar is unknown, and it only has the 3rd and 4th Regiments, with extremely weak strength. (August 6th)

Fierce Battle Against Bandits in Anyuan by the Southern Route Army 102

Headquarters of the Southern Route Army Established in Dayu

Guangzhou Communication: The Southern Route Bandit Suppression Army, with the 1st Army Commander concurrently serving as the 1st Column Commander, Yu Hanmou, held a military conference in Dayu a few days ago. Subsequently, the headquarters of the Southern Route Bandit Suppression Army was established, with Yu Hanmou concurrently serving as the director of the headquarters. The personnel of the headquarters are also concurrently filled by personnel from the 1st Army headquarters. The second phase of the communist suppression military operations is now actively underway. The 7th and 8th Divisions of the 2nd Column have been ordered to advance towards Junmenling. The 4th Division of the 1st Column, led by Zhang Meixin, and the 44th Division of the Guangxi Army, led by Wang Zanbin, encountered the main force of the communist bandits in the Zun San Wei area near Anyuan. The two sides engaged in an extremely fierce battle. Wang's division, led by Ling Moxie, besieged the communist bandits in the Zun San Wei area of the southern district of Anyuan for over ten days. One regiment of the bandit forces still stubbornly resisted with all their might. On the 28th and 29th of last month, over a thousand bandits, belonging to the pseudo-Workers' and Peasants' Red Army's 22nd Division, came from Huichang to reinforce them. They were fiercely attacked by Ling's regiment, resulting in the death of over 40 bandits. The bandits failed and retreated towards Huangbaikeng. On the 29th, approximately 4,000 people from the pseudo-Red Army's 3rd Division and the Independent 3rd Division, via the Dabatou area in the southeast of Anyuan, attempted to rescue the bandit forces in Zun San Wei. Wang's division then dispatched more troops, led by Mo Dehong's regiment, to launch a fierce attack on the bandits in cooperation with Ling's regiment. The intensity of the battle was unprecedented since Wang's division arrived in San Nan. As a result, over 600 bandits were killed, one pseudo-regimental commander and two pseudo-battalion commanders were wounded, and dozens of pseudo-company and platoon leaders died. The bandits could not withstand the attack and began to flee towards places such as Shahanzi at 10 PM. In this battle, Ling and Mo's regiments of Wang's division also suffered considerable losses. The following telegram was received yesterday from Division Commander Wang: (1) At Yinshi on the day of the incident, a phone call was received from Regiment Commander Mo from Zhenkou, stating that the bandits fighting against us, due to repeated violent衝鋒 towards us, were threatened by our intense firepower and suffered extraordinarily heavy casualties, resulting in a complete collapse of their front line around 10 PM last night (the 29th). (2) We have dispatched the Zhang, Tan, and Liu battalions to search towards Dabatou. (3) Wang Xisheng, the secretary of the 7th Regiment of the pseudo-3rd Division, and Li Qingshan, the messenger, surrendered to our regiment this morning with a machine gun. According to their testimony, they originally served in the 52nd Division of the Central Army, but were captured and forced to join the army. They came to Anyuan this time from Ruijin, belonging to the pseudo-3rd Division. The pseudo-Independent Division and the 3rd Division were originally in Anyuan. The pseudo-22nd Division came from Tingzhou. Each division had a strength of two regiments and three battalions, with four companies in each battalion, reaching over a hundred people, totaling over 6,000 people. They all had good rifles and claimed to be recovering Anyuan and Xunwu, but in reality, they were attempting to create disturbances. In this battle, each regiment suffered over 200 casualties. Due to the unfavorable situation, they scattered and fled towards Sanheshui and Guanpu last night. They took the opportunity to escape, etc. Furthermore, Wang Zanbin stated in a telegram one day that, according to the report from Deputy Division Commander Zhou Quan, troops were dispatched this morning to search the battlefield near Tubatou again. Each battalion returned to the Shiqiaotangdong area at 3 PM in the afternoon. Approximately 600 bandit corpses were abandoned along the way, with countless wounded. It is rumored that some scattered bandits are hiding in the forests, etc. (August 3rd)

Songjiang

Various Local Organizations Inspect Stored Grain 103

Last year, this county received an order to organize famine relief grain storage, collecting one jiao of silver per mu of land, collected along with the national tax, with separate receipts issued and collected, and a warehouse storage committee was established to purchase Xian grain and store it in separate warehouses. The committee sent a letter to the county government, requesting the Department of Civil Affairs to send personnel to Songjiang to inspect the grain in order to verify its accuracy. Subsequently, an order was received from the department, ordering compliance with Article 12 of the regulations for the management of local warehouses promulgated by the Ministry. Yesterday, the county government followed the regulations and invited representatives from local organizations, including County Magistrate Jin Tigan, Yang Zhimin from the County Chamber of Commerce, Li Xiuzhe from the Sijing Chamber of Commerce, Zhang Tianmin from the Tianma Chamber of Commerce, and warehouse committee members Ni Guangrong, Wu Qianmei, Wang Zhewu, Li Zuhua, and Zhang Siyong. County Magistrate Jin reported on the grain storage process, and then led the committee members and representatives to various warehouses to inspect the grain. It was verified that the original Xian grain, according to the Tanhu measurement, amounted to 1,849 shi and 5 dou, stored in eleven warehouses, which matched the numbers in the warehouse entry records. The grain was dry and showed no signs of pests, but needed to be frequently turned and aired for long-term storage.

Suzhou

Meeting to Expand Scout Plan 104

The Wu County Party and Government Joint Meeting decided on the first phase of the county's scout expansion plan: (1) Increase the number of scout troops by more than ten troops in addition to the existing number of troops; (2) Presumed organizing agencies: A. Schools: Dahu, Shangen, Caoqiao, Panhuan, Pingzhi, Pingjiang, Shengping, Xujiang, and other primary schools; B. Social organizations: Chamber of Commerce, Labor Union, Trade Association, etc.; (3) Funding: Schools will be funded by the Bureau of Education, and organizations will be allocated funds by their respective agencies. The minimum funding for each troop is as follows: A. Initial expenses (assuming two squads, 78 yuan): two tents, 50 yuan; two sets of cooking utensils, 10 yuan; twenty sticks, 5 yuan; camp stove, 3 yuan; totaling 78 yuan; B. Recurring expenses (excluding salaries): 15 yuan per semester; (4) Training talent: Schools may allow teachers with scout research to register and serve as trainers. Social organizations may request the Wu County Scout Council to delegate or send personnel for training; (5) Implementation period: August of this year. The Bureau of Education will order the relevant organizations to begin preparations. For preparation procedures, please have the Wu County Scout Council send personnel to assist in the process.

Wuxi

Rickshaw Pullers' Strike Calmed Down 105

The rickshaw trade association in this county revised the rickshaw rental fee to 3.7 jiao per rickshaw, which sparked a general strike by all rickshaw pullers in the county. Later, through fair mediation by both the Party and the government, they were persuaded to temporarily maintain the original state, and the situation slightly eased. Unexpectedly, the association freely issued a declaration of the importance of maintaining business operations, setting the standard at 4 jiao plus two copper coins. Therefore, the situation changed, and the rickshaw pullers still did not resume work. Later, the county government adopted decisive measures, such as immediately detaining and severely punishing rickshaw pullers who damaged rickshaws, and detaining and severely punishing rickshaw companies that did not release rickshaws or disrupted the trade, and also revoking their rickshaw licenses and ordering them to cease operations. After hearing the instructions, each rickshaw company and rickshaw puller immediately complied with the mediation intentions of the county magistrate, restored the usual practices, and agreed to resume work. At the same time, Qian Sunqing, the chairman of the Municipal Management Committee, believed that since the rickshaw trade association was preparing for reorganization, how could it arbitrarily convene a general meeting and collect rickshaw rentals of 3.7 jiao, seeking to implement a never-implemented proposal, inevitably taking advantage of the situation to please certain tradesmen and using it as a stepping stone for competitive elections. Yesterday, he specially sent a letter to the county government, requesting that the association, during the preparation for reorganization, should stop exercising its powers in accordance with customary practice, otherwise it should be dissolved to prevent someone from taking advantage of it and to quell local disputes. As for the rickshaw pullers intercepting rickshaws and coercing strikes, please strictly detain and punish them. Yesterday (8th) morning, the rickshaw pullers went to the rickshaw companies as usual to collect rickshaws and engaged in business peacefully. From Guangfu Gate to Jixiang Bridge Gongyun Bridge Railway Station, Wang Wei, the captain of the police brigade, and Wang Xiezhong, the chief of the second branch bureau in charge, ordered the police team to be armed and dispatched to maintain order. The rickshaw pullers were quiet as usual, quietly waiting for the Party and government to negotiate a compromise solution by the 16th of this month before resolving the matter again.

Key Suspect in Kidnapping Case Arrested in Beijing 106

Han Wentai, the head of Xu Xie Township in the third district of the county, was kidnapped by bandits and tragically murdered. The two suspects, Li Zhiping and Yuan Yonghe, were apprehended in Shanghai and have been brought to Wuxi for interrogation and detention. Five other suspects are still at large. One of the key suspects, Jiang Hanchen, escaped after being released on bail by the First Special District Court in Shanghai. He was recently found in Beijing by Jiang's uncle, Jin Pei, who apprehended him and handed him over to the Capital Police Department for custody. The Shanghai Special Court was notified by telegram. At that time, Wu Zhengrong, the Wuxi political and police chief, happened to be in Shanghai on official business. He immediately returned to Wuxi and reported to County Magistrate Yan to prepare a document and go to Beijing to welcome the suspects back for interrogation.

Changzhou

Eighteen-Year-Old Bandit Executed by Firing Squad 107

Previously, the Wu County Government received the bandit suspect Chen Xiaopei, who was handed over by the Public Security First Branch Bureau. Chen confessed that he was 18 years old and had participated in the robbery of Xu Shilin's store. When arrested, stolen goods were recovered, and the victim identified them in court without error. County Magistrate Cai, considering that the suspect and the stolen goods were both present and that there was a confirmed confession, proposed a death sentence. The proposal was submitted to the provincial government for approval and was immediately approved. At noon on the 7th, the police were dispatched to bring the suspect to the court to verify his identity, and he was tied up and taken to the Fengweidun execution ground to be executed by firing squad.

Main Perpetrator of Tangqiao Robbery Arrested 108

In the Mo Renrong robbery case in Tangqiao Township, Wu County, the previously apprehended suspect Qian Huolin died in prison due to illness. However, the main perpetrator in the case, Pan Jingou, had escaped and was not apprehended. Jin Wei, a patrol officer from the First Substation of the Public Security First Branch Bureau, recently received a report that the suspect was hiding in Baijiaqiao in the east gate. He immediately dispatched police to arrest him. After a preliminary trial, he was handed over to the county for interrogation on the afternoon of the 7th.

Yangzhou

Renkang Money Shop in Shaobo Robbed 109

The Renkang Money Shop in Damatou Town, Shaobo, which belongs to this county, was found to be as described, with prosperous business and a small savings department that also handled pawned gold and silverware. At around 8 PM on the 6th, two individuals suddenly entered, speaking with a Yancheng accent and wearing white cloth student uniforms, claiming to be exchanging foreign currency. They jumped into the counter, pulled out handguns, and threatened them not to make a sound. They ordered the manager, Cha Mingru, and the chief accountant, Kong Qi, to hand over the safe key. They then stole 107 yuan in paper money and 18 yuan in cash from the safe.

Gaoyou

Zhang Wenhua Tragically Murdered 110

Zhang Wenhua, who ran a livestock brokerage in Guagua Township, the tenth district of the county, was kidnapped by bandits at the beginning of last month and a ransom of 2,000 yuan was demanded. Zhang's family, finding it difficult to raise such a large sum of money at once, repeatedly pleaded with the bandits for an extension. This angered the bandits. On the evening of the 3rd, they tied Zhang up with ropes, dragged him to the front of his house, tied him to a willow tree, and shot him to death. They also stuck a paper flag on Zhang's body with the inscription "If other hostages do not prepare the ransom, they will be treated in the same way."

Rugao

Robbers Commit Robbery and Kidnap Child 111

In Xiaochenjia Village, Chenjia Township, Shizhuang District, Rugao, there is a Wu Gandie who is a farmer and has a relatively comfortable life. He is currently the head of the township. At around 12 AM last night, more than ten robbers suddenly came, holding guns and breaking down the door. They tied up Wu's entire family and stole all their clothes, silver coins, and jewelry, and also kidnapped a child. On the same day, a merchant was returning home from collecting accounts in a village called Kong Gang, east of Liujiazha. He was robbed of 160 yuan in accounts by two bandits, and his leg was shot by a bandit. Fortunately, it was not a vital area, and there was no danger to his life.

Filial Impiety Leads Elderly Woman to Suicide 112

In Daoshiguan, south of Guojiayuan, Shizhuang District, there is a Guo Kou who is addicted to tobacco and alcohol and does not engage in proper work. His mother, Wu, is already 77 years old. Because of her son's filial impiety, she had long harbored thoughts of ending her life. Last year, she attempted suicide behind people's backs because of an argument with her son, but it was unsuccessful. On the previous day (3rd), the mother and son suddenly had another argument over a minor matter. Wu thought to herself that she was over seventy years old and would die sooner or later. She secretly entered the change shed during lunchtime and hanged herself. By the time Guo Kou heard the news and went to save her, she had already stopped breathing. It was truly tragic.

Inspections of Palace Museum Furs Show No Damage 119

The Shanghai Office Will Host the Press Today

National News Agency reports that the Palace Museum's southward-bound antiquities were previously inspected by an organized temporary supervisory committee and found that some of the furs were slightly damp. It is now known that the office has requested fur experts to re-examine the furs, and the result is that they were not damaged. The Shanghai office of the museum has scheduled a reception for journalists this afternoon to publicly report. The details are recorded below:

Re-examination of Furs Shows No Damage 120

Zhou Huan, the chief of the office stationed in Shanghai by the museum, stated that when the boxes were opened previously, the furs were found to be damp, and a way should be found to dry them. However, for the sake of prudence, fur experts, Director Lu of the fur department of the Sincere Company, were specially invited to inspect them to determine the method. At 2 PM on the previous afternoon, the temporary supervisory committee was notified to send representatives to supervise the event, and Mr. Lu was invited to the ancient object storage location at 26 Tianzhutang Street. The two representatives of the supervisory committee and over ten assisting staff members were present. The treasurer, Cai Xianying, opened the vault and ordered the coolies to open the fur boxes. After Mr. Lu inspected them, the result was that he believed that there was no damage. The slight dampness previously discovered was because these furs were too old and tightly pressed in the boxes, causing a thin oil to be squeezed out of the leather, but this was a natural phenomenon and did not matter. It could not be considered dampness. Only four boxes were opened later, because they were all the same, so they were not opened further.

Reception for Journalists Today 121

The office of the museum stationed in Shanghai and the temporary supervisory committee are holding this inspection of antiquities. All sectors are paying close attention to them. Therefore, the supervisory committee previously resolved to regularly invite local journalists to publicly report. It is now known that a tea party has been scheduled for 3 PM this afternoon at the Yipinxiang Western Restaurant to invite all journalists in order to report on everything. It is heard that Ma Heng, the acting director of the museum, will also attend in person.

Deng's Department Sends Xu Yimin to Shanghai 126

Yesterday Morning He Went to Moganshan to Meet General Ma,

Reporting on the Death of Deng Wen

General Ma Zhanshan's anti-Japanese commander, Division Commander Deng Wen, was suddenly assassinated at dawn on the 31st of last month at his residence in Zhangjiakou. The sad news came, and General Ma was deeply saddened. Deng's department specially sent Mr. Xu Yimin as a representative to the south. He arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning and immediately went to Hangzhou to Moganshan to meet General Ma and report the truth. The Northeast News Agency reporter met with Mr. Xu yesterday. According to him, the details of Deng's anti-Japanese activities and the circumstances of his assassination were very detailed. The details are as follows:

Posthumous Photo of Deng Wen

Brief Biography of Deng Wen 127

Deng Wen, styled Xianzhang, was from Liaoning. He graduated from the Heilongjiang Military Academy, was intelligent and capable, and had extensive knowledge. After graduating, he served as the cavalry company commander in General Ma Zhanshan's department. Due to his loyalty to his duties, he was promoted to battalion commander. After the September 18th Incident, General Ma took the lead in the anti-Japanese resistance. Deng participated in the battle. During the Nenjiang Bridge Battle, he served as the cavalry regiment commander. During the Battle of Songpu, he was promoted to commander of the First Army by General Ma. Deng then led his troops to fight in Rehe and Chahar. The central government sent personnel to reorganize the troops and specially appointed him as the commander of the 10th Cavalry Division of the Vanguard Army, temporarily under the command of Liu Yifei. In total, Deng had followed General Ma for more than ten years, with outstanding achievements. His sudden assassination has caused deep mourning throughout the country.

Details of the Assassination 128

At dawn on the 31st of last month,

Deng was returning to his residence from a friend's place with two followers, only about half a mile away. Suddenly, seven people dressed in military uniforms, all carrying box cannons, followed Deng, about forty steps away. The thugs suddenly opened fire on Deng, firing thirty rounds in succession. Deng's followers were unable to return fire in time and failed to retaliate. Deng was shot seven times and died, a very tragic death. The murderers escaped on the spot. The cause of the assassination is unknown. Feng has allocated funds for the funeral and the arrest of the murderers after hearing the news. Deng's former position is now temporarily held by Tan Zixin.

Consoling Family Members 129

After Deng was assassinated, he left behind

more than thirty family members, all in Beiping. Deng's wife was heartbroken upon hearing the news. The former Director of Finance of Heilongjiang Province, Langguan Pu, also went to Moganshan to meet General Ma and report the situation. General Ma was deeply saddened and, out of consideration for Deng's past merits, immediately raised 5,000 yuan and remitted it to Shanghai for condolence.
